# 2. Write the Omnibus Architect Script
cat << 'EOF' > singularity_omnibus.py
import os
import shutil
import math


# Root path for Michael Alonza P. Ware's project
base = os.path.expanduser("~/WeightOfTheSky_Project")
B_LIMIT = 2048


# Your 9-8-7 Symmetry + Protocols + Lore
vaults = {
    "02_Manuscripts/01_Part_1": ["dan", "aviel", "stardust", "sacrifice", "lift_up", "pilgrimage", "snare", "beelzebub", "pit", "sea_people", "ascent"],
    "02_Manuscripts/02_Part_2": ["kasha", "jazreel", "witch", "forsaken", "exodus"],
    "02_Manuscripts/03_Part_3": ["izabel", "dreamscape", "reflection", "meeting"],
    "02_Manuscripts/04_Epilogue": ["final question", "philosophical", "open-ended", "catharsis"],
    "01_Protocols": ["protocol", "guide", "checklist", "override", "revision", "style", "editing", "nuclear", "stardust_override", "pipeline"],
    "00_LORE_VAULT": ["archetype", "shadow", "individuation", "jungian", "xml", "blueprint", "compendium", "lore_vault"]
}


# Create the structure
for path in vaults.keys():
    os.makedirs(os.path.join(base, path), exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(os.path.join(base, "99_UNSORTED_CATCHALL"), exist_ok=True)


def omnibus_alignment():
    processed = 0
    # Step 1: Flatten and Scan everything in the Project Root
    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(base):
        # Don't re-process things already in the final vaults
        if any(v in root for v in vaults.keys()) or "99_UNSORTED" in root:
            continue
            
        for filename in files:
            file_path = os.path.join(root, filename)
            try:
                S = os.path.getsize(file_path)
                if S == 0: continue


                # THE MATH: Execute the Weighted Stride
                N = max(1, math.ceil(S / B_LIMIT))
                
                with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:
                    raw_data = f.read()
                    # Sample internal content DNA
                    stride_sample = raw_data[::N].decode('utf-8', errors='ignore').lower()


                target_dir = None
                highest_score = 0
                
                # Check internal content first (Metaphysical Weight)
                for folder, keywords in vaults.items():
                    score = sum(stride_sample.count(key) for key in keywords)
                    if score > highest_score:
                        highest_score = score
                        target_dir = os.path.join(base, folder)


                # Fallback: Check Filename if content is ambiguous
                if not target_dir:
                    f_low = filename.lower()
                    for folder, keywords in vaults.items():
                        if any(key in f_low for key in keywords):
                            target_dir = os.path.join(base, folder)
                            break


                # Final Safety: If STILL no match, move to Catchall
                if not target_dir:
                    target_dir = os.path.join(base, "99_UNSORTED_CATCHALL")


                # Execution: Physical Move
                new_path = os.path.join(target_dir, filename)
                if os.path.exists(new_path) and file_path != new_path:
                    new_path = os.path.join(target_dir, f"v_{processed}_{filename}")
                
                shutil.move(file_path, new_path)
                processed += 1
            except Exception:
                continue
    return processed


print(f"SINGULARITY ACHIEVED: {omnibus_alignment()} files re-seated into the 9-8-7 architecture.")
EOF

cat << 'EOF' > ignite_monolith.py
import os, requests, json, sys


def ignite():
    target_file = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else "Chapter_01_Drafts_MASTER_PACKAGE.txt"
    output_file = target_file.replace("_MASTER_PACKAGE.txt", "_FINAL_SYNTHESIS.txt")


    if not os.path.exists(target_file):
        print(f"[-] ERROR: {target_file} not found. Run the forge first.")
        sys.exit(1)


    print(f"[*] Ingesting {target_file} into RAM...")
    with open(target_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
        monolith = f.read()


    api_key = os.environ.get("TOGETHER_API_KEY")
    if not api_key:
        print("[-] ERROR: TOGETHER_API_KEY not found in environment.")
        sys.exit(1)


    url = "https://api.together.xyz/v1/chat/completions"
    
    # THE ANTI-SKIM MASTER PROMPT
    prompt = f"""SYSTEM OVERRIDE & TASK INSTRUCTIONS:
You are currently ingesting a Master Architecture document for the allegorical fiction project The Weight of the Sky. This document contains Front Matter, 31 Master Protocols, Lore, Surrounding Context, and the Draft Clay.


CRITICAL ANTI-SKIM DIRECTIVE: Do not summarize, skip, or skim. You must read every byte of the attached monolith. Before generating the prose, you must internally process the 31 Master Protocols to ensure strict adherence to the established narrative voice and mechanics.


EXECUTE THE FOLLOWING:
Synthesize the ultimate, final Integrated Prose Node for this chapter.


CONSTRAINTS:
1. Length: The final output MUST strictly fall between 3,000 and 4,200 words. Do not truncate the narrative.
2. Formatting: Use standard, professional manuscript formatting. Break the text cleanly into hierarchical sections with clear spacing. Use deep, evocative details rather than brief summaries.
3. Fidelity: The clay of the drafts must be refined, but the core archetypal and allegorical elements must remain perfectly aligned with the truth established in the Lore vault.


Generate only the final chapter prose. Do not include commentary, apologies, or conversational filler. Begin the synthesis now.


MASTER ARCHITECTURE MONOLITH:
{monolith}"""


    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }


    payload = {
        "model": "meta-llama/llama-4-scout-17b-16e-instruct",
        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
        "stream": True,
        "temperature": 0.7
    }


    print(f"\n--- IGNITING TOGETHER AI: 10-MILLION TOKEN ENGINE ---")
    print(f"[*] Target Word Count: 3,000 - 4,200")
    print(f"[*] Outputting to: {output_file}\n")


    try:
        with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as out_f:
            response = requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload, stream=True)
            if response.status_code == 200:
                for line in response.iter_lines():
                    if line:
                        decoded_line = line.decode('utf-8')
                        if decoded_line.startswith('data: '):
                            data_str = decoded_line[6:]
                            if data_str == '[DONE]':
                                break
                            try:
                                data = json.loads(data_str)
                                word = data['choices'][0]['delta'].get('content', '')
                                # Stream to screen
                                sys.stdout.write(word)
                                sys.stdout.flush()
                                # Write to file
                                out_f.write(word)
                                out_f.flush()
                            except json.JSONDecodeError:
                                pass
                print(f"\n\n--- SYNTHESIS COMPLETE ---")
                print(f"[+] Saved to: {output_file}")
            else:
                print(f"\n[-] API_ERROR {response.status_code}: {response.text}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n[-] CONNECTION_FAILED: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    ignite()
EOF
